| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (9 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 9)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 9)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (9 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 9)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 9)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (9 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 9)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 9)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (8 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 8)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 8)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (8 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 8)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 8)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (7 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 7)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 7)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (7 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 7)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 7)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);

|     exit (1);

|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);

|       exit (0);

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| #include 
| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }
|

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (4 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 4)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 4)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (4 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 4)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 4)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (3 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 3)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 3)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (3 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 3)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 3)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }
|

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (3 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 3)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 3)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (2 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 2)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 2)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (2 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 2)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 2)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (2 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 2)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 2)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (1 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 1)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 1)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (1 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 1)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 1)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);

|     if (minor < 0)
|       exit (1);

|       exit (0);

|     exit (0);

|     exit (1);

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (0 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 0)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 0)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (major < 6)
|       exit (1);

|       exit (0);

|       exit (0);

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (9 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 9)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 9)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (9 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 9)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 9)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (9 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 9)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 9)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);

|       exit (0);

|     exit (0);

|     exit (1);

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (8 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 8)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 8)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (7 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 7)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 7)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (7 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 7)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 7)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (7 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 7)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 7)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }
|

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (6 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 6)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 6)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }
|

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (4 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 4)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 4)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (4 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 4)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 4)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }

| main ()
| {
|   int major, minor, patch;
| 
|   db_version(&major, &minor, &patch);
| 
|   /* Sanity check: ensure that db.h constants actually match the db library */
|   if (major != DB_VERSION_MAJOR
|       || minor != DB_VERSION_MINOR
|       || patch != DB_VERSION_PATCH)
|     exit (1);
| 
|   /* Run-time check:  ensure the library claims to be the correct version. */
| 
|   if (5 != -1) {
|     if (major < 5)
|       exit (1);
|     if (major > 5)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (4 != -1) {
|     if (minor < 4)
|       exit (1);
|     if (minor > 4)
|       exit (0);
|   }
| 
|   if (-1 == -1
|       || patch >= -1)
|     exit (0);
|   else
|     exit (1);
| }
